„ÄêMemory„Äë
"There are currently about 50 "InterContinental" brand hotels in **************, but there are only two InterContinental "executive apartments". One is Chengdu, and the other is Tianjin InterContinental, which I often stay in."

When the word "bao" is used in a place name, in most cases, it should be pronounced "pu (fourth tone)" instead of "bao", such as Shilibao in Beijing or Yujiabao in Tianjin Binhai New Area. so it is. This year marks the fifth anniversary of Tianjin InterContinental. Whether it is a birthday or a business, we Chinese people pay special attention to commemorating it every five or ten days. Therefore, staying at this hotel at such an important moment will have special commemorative significance .

„ÄêGuest room snapshot„Äë
"The living room in the suite is very large, suitable for me to work or memorize words."

The sunny side is very warm, especially when you wake up in the morning, it feels so warm and tender. During your stay, you can enjoy two snacks and a can of soft drink in the minibar, and a capsule coffee machine is standard.

„ÄêBrief introduction to the public area„Äë
"The ceiling on the left side of the first floor near the Financial Conference Center is great. There are also several classic cars on display, including the Rolls Royce from the 1970s, which is very suitable for car fans to take pictures."

The design of the corridors in the guest room area is similar to the hollowed-out patios of InterContinental Hangzhou and Vientiane Tiancheng Holiday in Shijiazhuang, and the entire hollowed-out area of ‚Äã‚Äãthis InterContinental, if you overlook it, looks like the shell logo of InterContinental. Such a caring Chinese owner is rare. up. I live in 1166 hotels. I am the professional car host who has hosted the Tianjin Auto Show the most times in China. I don‚Äôt know how many times I have hosted it since 2006. In addition, I often come to Tianjin to host various real estate, automobile, and high-end wedding ceremonies. Waiting for events, so I still know the hotels in Tianjin very well, including this InterContinental, which has stayed too many times (lived in when it first opened), and often hosts performances here, after all, it is integrated with the Financial Conference Center Yes, especially suitable for holding meetings.

„ÄêBreakfast Overview„Äë
"Breakfast is very rich, it's on the first floor, and Caifenglou (the Chinese food brand of InterContinental Group, the big one is called Caifenglou, and the small one is called Caifeng Restaurant, which are widely distributed in InterContinental, Hualuxe, Crowne Plaza, etc., It has become one of IHG's local cultural signs), and the executive club is next to each other."

When you come to Tianjin, you must try the pancakes. The pancakes for breakfast at this restaurant are not bad. Mr. Guo Degang said that if you eat breakfast in Tianjin for two consecutive months, you will not bring heavy samples. Another thing worth recommending is its beef noodles, which are made with real ingredients. Those who don‚Äôt know it think it‚Äôs in the Northwest. Of course, raw porridge is also very authentic.

„ÄêMember Privileges„Äë

There are welcome desserts, welcome fruits, welcome drink coupons, peace of mind bags, exquisite tea gift boxes, and breakfast bags (picnic bags). The executive club has a rich set of meals, with a wide variety of seafood and sushi, and the desserts can actually be richer. In the past, the hotel would send back the things I missed in the guest room for free, but I still need to pay for the postage when I find something in this store. It‚Äôs so cute.
